1413 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 112:
1414 \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a690504b662e4281515bf12722df178ba}{YY\_RULE\_SETUP}
1415 \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_aad1dc60a04a1d8cfc8b3ded13601e361}{ECHO};
1416     \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a3cc40a460ad7df816678bcc05241e84c}{YY\_BREAK}
1417 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ab3077e60914fc54dcc55ecae1ce9700b}{YY\_STATE\_EOF}(\hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_aa3d063564f6ab16f6d408b8369d0e9ff}{INITIAL}):
1418 case YY\_STATE\_EOF(\hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a205b41db7d62b73142b0cf8e5d7d28a2}{MAPC}):
1419     \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ac3286b18a2e91b4571b97df96a118e84}{yyterminate}();
1420 
1421     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ab2708fd42cff29ce6a0a52b91bea40d1}{YY\_END\_OF\_BUFFER}:
1422         \{
1423         \textcolor{comment}{/* Amount of text matched not including the EOB char. */}
1424         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yy\_amount\_of\_matched\_text = (int) (yy\_cp - \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a790a191a93ef4d3b8c0bb43fd7480052}{yytext\_ptr}) - 1;
1425 
1426         \textcolor{comment}{/* Undo the effects of YY\_DO\_BEFORE\_ACTION. */}
1427         *yy\_cp = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a13f78e763996d2d86c85b45cbe146282}{yy\_hold\_char};
1428 
1429         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a38d4b4b5964f7d49b4d9e19bf81996df}{yy\_current\_buffer}->\hyperlink{structyy__buffer__state_a70fd925d37a2f0454fbd0def675d106c}{yy\_buffer\_status} == 
      \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a53579db42834b88199458993912c646d}{YY\_BUFFER\_NEW} )
1430             \{
1431             \textcolor{comment}{/* We're scanning a new file or input source.  It's}
1432 \textcolor{comment}{             * possible that this happened because the user}
1433 \textcolor{comment}{             * just pointed yyin at a new source and called}
1434 \textcolor{comment}{             * yylex().  If so, then we have to assure}
1435 \textcolor{comment}{             * consistency between yy\_current\_buffer and our}
1436 \textcolor{comment}{             * globals.  Here is the right place to do so, because}
1437 \textcolor{comment}{             * this is the first action (other than possibly a}
1438 \textcolor{comment}{             * back-up) that will match for the new input source.}
1439 \textcolor{comment}{             */}
1440             \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_aa86c122f2050dbfd365fcf547e6fc1c3}{yy\_n\_chars} = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a38d4b4b5964f7d49b4d9e19bf81996df}{yy\_current\_buffer}->
      \hyperlink{structyy__buffer__state_a06406208824817acfec2183b79080945}{yy\_n\_chars};
1441             \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a38d4b4b5964f7d49b4d9e19bf81996df}{yy\_current\_buffer}->\hyperlink{structyy__buffer__state_a4360acfb226a1fc240ab2be17dd6beda}{yy\_input\_file} = 
      \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a46af646807e0797e72b6e8945e7ea88b}{yyin};
1442             \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a38d4b4b5964f7d49b4d9e19bf81996df}{yy\_current\_buffer}->\hyperlink{structyy__buffer__state_a70fd925d37a2f0454fbd0def675d106c}{yy\_buffer\_status} = 
      \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a609d19f40900ecc2a5f812d9388c21fb}{YY\_BUFFER\_NORMAL};
1443             \}
1444 
1445         \textcolor{comment}{/* Note that here we test for yy\_c\_buf\_p "<=" to the position}
1446 \textcolor{comment}{         * of the first EOB in the buffer, since yy\_c\_buf\_p will}
1447 \textcolor{comment}{         * already have been incremented past the NUL character}
1448 \textcolor{comment}{         * (since all states make transitions on EOB to the}
1449 \textcolor{comment}{         * end-of-buffer state).  Contrast this with the test}
1450 \textcolor{comment}{         * in input().}
1451 \textcolor{comment}{         */}
1452         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( yy\_c\_buf\_p <= &yy\_current\_buffer->yy\_ch\_buf[\hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_aa86c122f2050dbfd365fcf547e6fc1c3}{yy\_n\_chars}] )
1453             \{ \textcolor{comment}{/* This was really a NUL. */}
1454             \hyperlink{dgn__lex_8c_a9ba7c416f135b0f0c1f4addded4616b5}{yy\_state\_type} yy\_next\_state;
1455 
1456             \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ade8fc57d3529bff56440a4f3e9c29586}{yy\_c\_buf\_p} = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a790a191a93ef4d3b8c0bb43fd7480052}{yytext\_ptr} + yy\_amount\_of\_matched\_text;
1457 
1458             yy\_current\_state = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ac7941891fb35553e85c394d7240b6fac}{yy\_get\_previous\_state}();
1459 
1460             \textcolor{comment}{/* Okay, we're now positioned to make the NUL}
1461 \textcolor{comment}{             * transition.  We couldn't have}
1462 \textcolor{comment}{             * yy\_get\_previous\_state() go ahead and do it}
1463 \textcolor{comment}{             * for us because it doesn't know how to deal}
1464 \textcolor{comment}{             * with the possibility of jamming (and we don't}
1465 \textcolor{comment}{             * want to build jamming into it because then it}
1466 \textcolor{comment}{             * will run more slowly).}
1467 \textcolor{comment}{             */}
1468 
1469             yy\_next\_state = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_aef834b9da0e6ab2c8100976ec1ebd004}{yy\_try\_NUL\_trans}( yy\_current\_state );
1470 
1471             yy\_bp = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a790a191a93ef4d3b8c0bb43fd7480052}{yytext\_ptr} + \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a68792d73820bc46a71d3d4e613f0b977}{YY\_MORE\_ADJ};
1472 
1473             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( yy\_next\_state )
1474                 \{
1475                 \textcolor{comment}{/* Consume the NUL. */}
1476                 yy\_cp = ++\hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ade8fc57d3529bff56440a4f3e9c29586}{yy\_c\_buf\_p};
1477                 yy\_current\_state = yy\_next\_state;
1478                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} yy\_match;
1479                 \}
1480 
1481             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
1482                 \{
1483                 yy\_cp = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ade8fc57d3529bff56440a4f3e9c29586}{yy\_c\_buf\_p};
1484                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} yy\_find\_action;
1485                 \}
1486             \}
1487 
1488         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} ( \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a941fbfdbb3a4aa1ebc5bbac0be477d2d}{yy\_get\_next\_buffer}() )
1489             \{
1490             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a7f71d7fa2c403eb4b2f38cb9536f3c63}{EOB\_ACT\_END\_OF\_FILE}:
1491                 \{
1492                 \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a57edb4569f96dcfce9deaff0eb6a6412}{yy\_did\_buffer\_switch\_on\_eof} = 0;
1493 
1494                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( \hyperlink{dgn__main_8c_ad35c8efbce4ce6e59d2b4be1d6865e31}{yywrap}() )
1495                     \{
1496                     \textcolor{comment}{/* Note: because we've taken care in}
1497 \textcolor{comment}{                     * yy\_get\_next\_buffer() to have set up}
1498 \textcolor{comment}{                     * yytext, we can now set up}
1499 \textcolor{comment}{                     * yy\_c\_buf\_p so that if some total}
1500 \textcolor{comment}{                     * hoser (like flex itself) wants to}
1501 \textcolor{comment}{                     * call the scanner after we return the}
1502 \textcolor{comment}{                     * YY\_NULL, it'll still work - another}
1503 \textcolor{comment}{                     * YY\_NULL will get returned.}
1504 \textcolor{comment}{                     */}
1505                     \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ade8fc57d3529bff56440a4f3e9c29586}{yy\_c\_buf\_p} = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a790a191a93ef4d3b8c0bb43fd7480052}{yytext\_ptr} + \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a68792d73820bc46a71d3d4e613f0b977}{YY\_MORE\_ADJ};
1506 
1507                     yy\_act = \hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_ab3077e60914fc54dcc55ecae1ce9700b}{YY\_STATE\_EOF}(\hyperlink{lev__lex_8c_a8e14785f9eab7a997d659b25af9584c5}{YY\_START});
